home
Hi all, this is the forum where you can find and share level codes, to play each other's levels.

To Share your code, scroll to the bottom of the page, paste your code into the text box, and click Submit.
Make sure you verified your code before attempting to share.

Please do not edit your code, as they are formatted to make them easy to share and view. Just paste and submit.

To Copy a code, you only need the data in the box, Do Not Copy the Title or Description.
Simply triple click the code until it all highlights, then right click it and click ‘Copy’, or click CTRL + C. Then, from the game's Title Screen, click Load Level and paste your code.

Please do not share anything that may violate Community Guidelines. If you want to talk about someone's level, please quote that level so others don't need to search for the one you're talking about. Feel free to make posts with multiple codes, or to repost a level code that you enjoyed, but do not repost one multiple times.

If your post does not include a Level Code, do not post it.

Link to the game: https://scratch.mit.edu/projects/556047373

If you see someone reposting, advertising, spamming, or posting something unrelated to the topic, report their message.
Keeping this topic clean will make it much easier to use. Enjoy the game.

If you're looking for something in particular, use this site to search:
https://ocular.jeffalo.net/search?q=%2Btopic%3A%22536337%22%20%20%2Bcontent%3A%22SEARCH%20HERE%22&sort=relevance
Just replace the SEARCH HERE part of the search bar with what you want to search for, e.g: Auto.
Using the other features will also allow you to search for certain user's levels and filter by time posted.

If you want to make a level but don't know what you should make, you could try making: a classic style level, an auto level, a puzzle level, a level made with only a few items, a remake of an official level, a speed run level, or look at what others have made for ideas.
